<review>I LOVE this place.  Every person that works there is pleasant and knowledgable, and I know that my babies are being taken care of. After only a couple of visits, the people there would call him by name as we walked in the door. Our corgi, Luigi, goes there now for day visits just to socialize with the other dogs. There aren't any toys, but it's a good thing-plus, they don't need them. my dog loves to play with other dogs, but get a toy involved and he's like a bratty child. ALL of the dogs have access to the outside, but any accidents that happen inside are cleaned up almost immediately (I know this because I take advantage of the webcams that are placed in each section).

We also board our dogs there (corgi and chihuahua). I love the amenites that can be added. We always add a kong treat for each night, a little extra one-on-one time, and a bath and nail trim to the end of Luigi's overnight stays. He comes home trimmed and smelling wonderful. This last time we also added a  reiki massage to Luigi's stay, and received a one-page handwritten note about his experience. I also like that your dogs can be boarded together for a cheaper price.

It is unfortunate that not all breeds are accepted, but this has nothing to do with how knowledgable the staff is. Places like this deal with a lot of dogs...and a lot of dog owners (which I would guess is why they don't accept certain breeds).

You'll never please everyone, but as a dog lover, I personally will never go anywhere else!<//review><Pictures>None< /Pictures><response>None</response><GmapID>0x54d1555e5464711b:0x25bb75d11f29d161< /GmapID></record>

< Review>
If you love flavorful and hot Chinese dishes, you've come to the right place. A solid majority of the menu boasts some level of spice, although they do have enough non-spicy options for anyone in your party who can't handle any heat. Everything we ordered was tasty, and I would happily order most of the entrees again: cumin lamb, steamed fresh sea bass, beef in hot chili oil, eggplant in garlic sauce, couple beef, and walnut shrimp. The shrimp fried rice and Hunan crispy noodles were good too, but they served mainly to balance the strong flavors of the rest of the meal. My favorite dishes were the cumin lamb, the beef in hot chili sauce, and the walnut shrimp. Service was excellent, and except for the longer wait for the steamed fresh fish, food came out very quickly during our Sunday lunch. Would recommend.</Review>

< Review>
(Translated by Google) I came here for lunch on a Thursday and Saturday. Saturday menu is fancier with lots of pictures. And more expensive. Satisfied with everything, especially the frog. Very juicy and fresh. I asked for light spicy and it was still a little bit beyond my level. Still, extremely good.
Update 1/13/2020: Yes they have upgraded the menu, and price 2-3 dollars higher than previously..
Noon each Thursday and Saturday to a Saturday richer menu, each dish is also expensive on 1-4 dollars. Frog two points are very good, pickled frog a little too spicy for me. Very fresh fullness q shells. The second point Griddle frog requires less spicy, served just when the spiciness just right for me, a little hemp flavor, very, very good.
Lettuce twice-cooked pork is not bad, but not lettuce fresh lettuce, lettuce is dry. Celery Xianggan too reactive, but as long as the $ 9.95 that day is very real.
January 2020 Update: Upgrade menu, price increases friends.

(Original)
I came here for lunch on a Thursday and Saturday. Saturday menu is fancier with lots of pictures. And more expensive. Satisfied with everything, especially the frog. Very juicy and fresh. I asked for light spicy and it was still a little bit beyond my level. Still, extremely good.
Update 1/13/2020: Yes they have upgraded the menu, and price. 2-3 dollars higher than previously.

By the late afternoon, my husband was no longer in any pain. We never did get a call back from our former dentist, so we just kept going to this office. Over the years there have been several dentists who have rotated through this office. I have seen some reviews about this office complaining about long wait times.
